                    random: true,
                    anim: {
                        enable: false,
                        speed: 40,
                        size_min: 0.1,
                        sync: false
                    }
                },
                line_linked: { 
                    enable: true, 
                    distance: 150, 
                
```

                    attract: {
                        enable: false,
                        rotateX: 600
```

                    out_mode: 'out', 
                    bounce: false,

                        rotateY: 1200
                    }
                }
            },

                detect_on: 'canvas',
                events: { 
                    onhover:

                    direction: 'none', 
                    random: false, 
                    straight: false, 
                    out_mode: 'out', 
                    bounce: false,
                    attract: {
                        enable: false,
                        rotateX: 600,
                        rotateY: 1200
                    }
                }
            },
            interactivity: {
                detect_on: 'canvas',
                events: { 
                    onhover: { 
                        enable: true, 
                        mode: 'repulse' 
                    }, 
                    onclick: { 
                        enable: true, 
                        mode: 'push' 
                    }, 
                    resize: true 
                },
                modes: {
```

0.4, 
                    width: 1 
                },
                move: { 
                    enable: true, 
                    speed: 2, 
                    direction: 'none', 
                    random: false, 
                    straight: false, 
                    out_mode: 'out', 
                    bounce: false,
                    attract: {
                        enable: false,
                        rotateX: 600,
                        rotateY: 1200
                    }
                }
            },

                detect_on: 'canvas',
                events: { 
                    onhover: { 
                        enable: true, 
                        mode: 'repulse' 
                    }, 
                    onclick: { 
                        enable: true, 
                        mode: 'push' 
                    },

                },

                            opacity: 1
                        }
                    },

```
0.4, 
                    width: 1 
                },
                move: { 
                    enable: true, 
                    speed: 2, 
                    direction: 'none', 
                    random: false, 
                    straight: false, 
                    out_mode: 'out', 
                    bounce: false,
                    attract: {
                        enable: false,
                        rotateX: 600,
                        rotateY: 1200
                    }
                }
            },
            interactivity: {
                detect_on: 'canvas',
                events: { 
                    onhover: { 
                        enable: true, 
                        mode: 'repulse' 
                    }, 
                    onclick: { 
                        enable: true, 
                        mode: 'push' 
                    }, 
                    resize: true 
                },
                modes: { 
                    grab: {
                        distance: 400,
                        line_linked: {
                            opacity: 1
                        }
                    },
                    bubble: {
                        distance: 400,
                        size: 40,
                        
```

                detect_on: 'canvas',
                events: { 
                    onhover: { 
                        enable: true, 
                        mode: 'repulse' 
                    }, 
                    onclick: { 
                        enable: true, 
                        mode: 'push' 
                    }, 
                    resize: true 
                },
                modes: { 
                    grab: {
                        distance: 400,
                        line_linked: {
                            opacity: 1
                        }
                    },
                    bubble: {
                        distance: 400,
                        size: 40,
                        duration: 2,
                        opacity: 8,
                        speed: 3
                    },
```

                        distance: 400,
                        line_linked: {
                            opacity: 1
                        }
                    },
                    bubble: {
                        distance: 400,
                        size: 40,
                        duration: 2,
                        opacity: 8,
                        speed: 3
                    },
                    repulse: {
                        distance: 200,
                        duration: 0.
```

                    enable: true, 
                    speed: 2, 
                    direction: 'none', 
                    random: false, 
                    straight: false, 
                    out_mode: 'out', 
                    bounce: false,
                    attract: {
                        enable: false,
                        rotateX: 600,
                        rotateY: 1200
                    }
                }
            },
            interactivity: {
                detect_on: 'canvas',
                events: { 
                    onhover: { 
                        enable: true, 
                        mode: 'repulse' 
                    }, 
                    onclick: { 
                        enable: true, 
                        mode: 'push' 
                    }, 
                    resize: true 
                },
                modes: { 
                    grab: {
                        distance: 400,
                        line_linked: {
                            opacity: 1
                        }
                    },
                    bubble: {
                        distance: 400,
                        size: 40,
                        duration: 2,
                        opacity: 8,
                        speed: 3
                    },
                    repulse: {
                        distance: 200,
                        duration: 0.4
                    },
                    push: { 
                        particles_nb: 4 
                    },
                    remove: {
```

                        size: 40,
                        duration: 2,

                    },

                    },

                    }
                }

scrolling for navigation links
        document.querySelectorAll('a[href^="#"]').forEach(anchor => {
            anchor.addEventListener('click', function (e) {
                e.preventDefault();
                const target = document.querySelector(this.getAttribute('href'));
                if (target) {
                    target.scrollIntoView({
                        behavior: 'smooth',
                        block: 'start'
                    });
                }
```
